pipeline is implemented across multiple C++ source files in the gecko-dev repository. The pipeline consists of three main components:\\n\\n**1. Frame Construction (nsCSSFrameConstructor)**\\nFrame construction is managed by nsCSSFrameConstructor.cpp/h located in layout/base/. This class is responsible for constructing the frame tree from the DOM tree based on CSS display properties. Key methods handle ContentAppended, ContentInserted, and frame reconstruction for style changes. The FrameConstructionItem and FrameConstructionData structures guide how frames should be created.\\n\\n**2. Block Layout Reflow Pipeline**\\nThe block layout reflow is the core of the layout engine:\\n\\n- **PresShell (layout/base/PresShell.cpp/h)**: The presentation shell is the main entry point for layout. It orchestrates the overall reflow process through methods like DoReflow() and manages dirty frames via FrameNeedsReflow().\\n\\n- **nsBlockFrame (layout/generic/nsBlockFrame.cpp/h)**: The primary block container frame implementation. The Reflow() method performs the actual block layout, handling floats, margins, and child frame positioning.\\n\\n- **BlockReflowState (layout/generic/BlockReflowState.cpp/h)**: Maintains state during block reflow including float tracking, margin collapsing, and available space calculations.\\n\\n- **nsBlockReflowContext (layout/generic/nsBlockReflowContext.cpp/h)**: Helper class for reflowing block frames, handling block-level child frames and their positioning.\\n\\n- **nsLineLayout (layout/generic/nsLineLayout.cpp/h)**: Manages inline content layout within lines. Handles span management, baseline calculations, and inline frame positioning. The ReflowFrame() method processes individual frames within a line.\\n\\n- **nsLineBox (layout/generic/nsLineBox.cpp/h)**: Represents a line of inline content with cached metrics and dirty state. The line list (nsLineList) maintains all lines in a block.\\n\\n- **ReflowInput/ReflowOutput (layout/generic/ReflowInput.cpp/h and ReflowOutput.cpp/h)**: Core data structures carrying reflow parameters (input constraints, spacing, etc.) and results (computed sizes, metrics, overflow areas).\\n\\n**3. Dirty Frame Invalidation Mechanism**\\nDirty frame tracking and invalidation is managed through several interconnected systems:\\n\\n- **Frame State Management (nsFrameState.cpp/h, nsFrameStateBits.h)**: Bit flags on frames track dirty states including NS_FRAME_IS_DIRTY, NS_FRAME_HAS_DIRTY_CHILDREN, and NS_FRAME_NEEDS_REFLOW. These bits are checked and updated during reflow.\\n\\n- **nsIFrame Invalidation Methods (nsIFrame.cpp/h)**: Base frame class provides methods for invalidating frames and their subtrees. Methods like ChildIsDirty() in nsBlockFrame detect which children need reflow.\\n\\n- **Dirty Line Marking (nsBlockFrame.cpp)**: nsBlockFrame::LazyMarkLinesDirty() marks lines as dirty when needed. nsBlockFrame::ChildIsDirty() handles invalidation when child frames change.\\n\\n- **RestyleManager (layout/style/RestyleManager.cpp/h)**: Handles style invalidation that triggers reflow. ProcessAllPendingAttributeAndStateInvalidations() drives style-based dirty frame propagation.\\n\\n**Supporting Components**\\n\\nThe pipeline also includes specialized layout systems:\\n\\n- **Float Management (nsFloatManager.cpp/h)**: Tracks float positioning and available space around floats during line layout.\\n\\n- **Table Layout (layout/tables/)**: nsTableFrame, nsTableRowFrame, nsTableCellFrame, nsTableRowGroupFrame handle table-specific layout with specialized reflow logic.\\n\\n- **Flex/Grid Layout (nsFlexContainerFrame.cpp/h, nsGridContainerFrame.cpp/h)**: Modern layout algorithms using specialized reflow input/output.\\n\\n- **Inline Frame Handling (nsInlineFrame.cpp/h, nsFirstLetterFrame.cpp/h)**: Special inline container and pseudo-element handling.\\n\\n- **Printing Support (nsPageFrame, nsPageContentFrame, nsPageSequenceFrame)**: Paginated layout for print and preview modes.\\n\\nThe reflow pipeline executes through a top-down traversal starting from PresShell::DoReflow(), which initiates block reflow via nsBlockFrame::Reflow(). Each frame type implements the Reflow() virtual method accepting ReflowInput and returning ReflowOutput. Dirty frames are marked and processed incrementally, with RestyleManager triggering invalidations based on style changes detected through the Servo style system.\"\n}\n"},"caller":{"type":"direct"}}],"stop_reason":null,"stop_sequence":null,"usage":{"input_tokens":7,"cache_creation_input_tokens":2387,"cache_read_input_tokens":99532,"cache_creation":{"ephemeral_5m_input_tokens":0,"ephemeral_1h_input_tokens":2387},"output_tokens":1,"service_tier":"standard","inference_geo":"not_available"},"context_management":null},"parent_tool_use_id":null,"session_id":"5a2ee4c3-0aba-4fa2-a493-eefdbb590018","uuid":"6233c6dc-ae80-4aa4-b2ba-b03d0ab752ae"}

pipeline is implemented across multiple C++ source files in the gecko-dev repository. The pipeline consists of three main components:\\n\\n**1. Frame Construction (nsCSSFrameConstructor)**\\nFrame construction is managed by nsCSSFrameConstructor.cpp/h located in layout/base/. This class is responsible for constructing the frame tree from the DOM tree based on CSS display properties. Key methods handle ContentAppended, ContentInserted, and frame reconstruction for style changes. The FrameConstructionItem and FrameConstructionData structures guide how frames should be created.\\n\\n**2. Block Layout Reflow Pipeline**\\nThe block layout reflow is the core of the layout engine:\\n\\n- **PresShell (layout/base/PresShell.cpp/h)**: The presentation shell is the main entry point for layout. It orchestrates the overall reflow process through methods like DoReflow() and manages dirty frames via FrameNeedsReflow().\\n\\n- **nsBlockFrame (layout/generic/nsBlockFrame.cpp/h)**: The primary block container frame implementation. The Reflow() method performs the actual block layout, handling floats, margins, and child frame positioning.\\n\\n- **BlockReflowState (layout/generic/BlockReflowState.cpp/h)**: Maintains state during block reflow including float tracking, margin collapsing, and available space calculations.\\n\\n- **nsBlockReflowContext (layout/generic/nsBlockReflowContext.cpp/h)**: Helper class for reflowing block frames, handling block-level child frames and their positioning.\\n\\n- **nsLineLayout (layout/generic/nsLineLayout.cpp/h)**: Manages inline content layout within lines. Handles span management, baseline calculations, and inline frame positioning. The ReflowFrame() method processes individual frames within a line.\\n\\n- **nsLineBox (layout/generic/nsLineBox.cpp/h)**: Represents a line of inline content with cached metrics and dirty state. The line list (nsLineList) maintains all lines in a block.\\n\\n- **ReflowInput/ReflowOutput (layout/generic/ReflowInput.cpp/h and ReflowOutput.cpp/h)**: Core data structures carrying reflow parameters (input constraints, spacing, etc.) and results (computed sizes, metrics, overflow areas).\\n\\n**3. Dirty Frame Invalidation Mechanism**\\nDirty frame tracking and invalidation is managed through several interconnected systems:\\n\\n- **Frame State Management (nsFrameState.cpp/h, nsFrameStateBits.h)**: Bit flags on frames track dirty states including NS_FRAME_IS_DIRTY, NS_FRAME_HAS_DIRTY_CHILDREN, and NS_FRAME_NEEDS_REFLOW. These bits are checked and updated during reflow.\\n\\n- **nsIFrame Invalidation Methods (nsIFrame.cpp/h)**: Base frame class provides methods for invalidating frames and their subtrees. Methods like ChildIsDirty() in nsBlockFrame detect which children need reflow.\\n\\n- **Dirty Line Marking (nsBlockFrame.cpp)**: nsBlockFrame::LazyMarkLinesDirty() marks lines as dirty when needed. nsBlockFrame::ChildIsDirty() handles invalidation when child frames change.\\n\\n- **RestyleManager (layout/style/RestyleManager.cpp/h)**: Handles style invalidation that triggers reflow. ProcessAllPendingAttributeAndStateInvalidations() drives style-based dirty frame propagation.\\n\\n**Supporting Components**\\n\\nThe pipeline also includes specialized layout systems:\\n\\n- **Float Management (nsFloatManager.cpp/h)**: Tracks float positioning and available space around floats during line layout.\\n\\n- **Table Layout (layout/tables/)**: nsTableFrame, nsTableRowFrame, nsTableCellFrame, nsTableRowGroupFrame handle table-specific layout with specialized reflow logic.\\n\\n- **Flex/Grid Layout (nsFlexContainerFrame.cpp/h, nsGridContainerFrame.cpp/h)**: Modern layout algorithms using specialized reflow input/output.\\n\\n- **Inline Frame Handling (nsInlineFrame.cpp/h, nsFirstLetterFrame.cpp/h)**: Special inline container and pseudo-element handling.\\n\\n- **Printing Support (nsPageFrame, nsPageContentFrame, nsPageSequenceFrame)**: Paginated layout for print and preview modes.\\n\\nThe reflow pipeline executes through a top-down traversal starting from PresShell::DoReflow(), which initiates block reflow via nsBlockFrame::Reflow(). Each frame type implements the Reflow() virtual method accepting ReflowInput and returning ReflowOutput. Dirty frames are marked and processed incrementally, with RestyleManager triggering invalidations based on style changes detected through the Servo style system.\"\n}\n","structuredPatch":[],"originalFile":null}}
